  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_8028077f-c173-4b52-b6cd-b94df8854c5b'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

<div id="review_468356359" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/468356359" />
    <a title="Jordan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13694166-jordan"><img alt="Jordan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515280240p2/13694166.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/468356359?book_show_action=true">Dec 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jordan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jordan" href="/user/show/13694166-jordan">Jordan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13694166-jordan?shelf=did-not-finish">did-not-finish</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13694166-jordan?shelf=2012">2012</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer468356359" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15871767352477204055"><i>Mile High</i> is <i>Fifty Shades</i> fanfic gone wrong. Let me provide a brief synopsis of this book: Bianca and James have sex. Yep, that’s it. No character development. No storyline. No plot. Just sex – straight up book porn. Which might serve its purpose if it was hot sex, however, sometimes <i>Mile High</i> sex ventured a bit too much into weird territory. Let me explain.<br/><br/>I personally enjoy a good, kinky BDSM book. I loved The Original Sinners series, which has tons of hot, smexy, kinky scenes. However, there </span>
  <span id="freeText15871767352477204055" style="display:none"><i>Mile High</i> is <i>Fifty Shades</i> fanfic gone wrong. Let me provide a brief synopsis of this book: Bianca and James have sex. Yep, that’s it. No character development. No storyline. No plot. Just sex – straight up book porn. Which might serve its purpose if it was hot sex, however, sometimes <i>Mile High</i> sex ventured a bit too much into weird territory. Let me explain.<br /><br />I personally enjoy a good, kinky BDSM book. I loved The Original Sinners series, which has tons of hot, smexy, kinky scenes. However, there is a difference between hot/kinky and just plain weird. In fact, let’s play a game of “Hot or Not” with <i>Mile High</i>:<br /><br /><i> “We’re going to fuck like animals in the horse stalls, and you’re going to love it” </i> – James <br /><b> Hot or Not? </b> Not really that hot. Kinda weird.<br /><br /><i> “I’m going to drink your milk like this when you breastfeed our children” </i> – James <br /><b> Hot or Not? </b> NOT. WTF.<br /><br /><i> “I sucked in a breath as he nuzzled into my underarm, licking me there as though it were a rare treat.” </i> <br /><b> Hot or Not? </b> No. Gross.<br /><br />Also, the author completely rips off an entire sex scene from <i>Fifty Shades</i>. Remember, the feather/flogging scene in which Christian plays <i>Spem in Alium</i>? (Clearly I do) Yeah, exact same sex scene in this book. James even turns on “soft, dark, ominous” music. Not cool.<br /><br />Moving on… I liked a couple things about the first book, but these good aspects disappeared in the second. Stephan barely played any part in this book. Where did her father go? Did he just magically disappear? Maintaining that part of the story could have made this book more interesting. The fact that Bianca enjoyed being a submissive was interesting but not explored. About 60% James does explore this by teaching Bianca a lesson (I’m being intentionally vague here so as not to spoil anything). I found this part to be enjoyable, yet short-lived.<br /><br />Typically, the main character can make or break any book for the reader, which may have also contributed to my distaste. Bianca really started to grate my nerves in the second book. She constantly refused to discuss ANY of her feelings or emotions. I accepted this in the first book but it just became really annoying this time around. James constantly showed how much he cared for her. He created a book shelf in his library just for her, he purchased clothes for her in each of his houses so she would never need to worry, he dedicated an entire room to her so she could paint, he asked her to move in. The list goes on and on. Yet, somehow, she still felt like he only wanted her for sex for a short period. How dense can you be? Seriously. It became ridiculous. Her constant obsession with his past became annoying as well. <br /><br />This book appeals to one type of person only - someone interested in reading Fifty Shades fanfiction. I have already read Fifty Shades, twice actually, so I would prefer something new and original. I had to DNF this at about 86% in.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15871767352477204055" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer456488979" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2506069595485050908">This is another deeply erotic and highly emotional instalment in Bianca and James' story.<br/><br/>It's the second part of the Up in the Air Trilogy and it doesn’t work as a standalone. You need to read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16134782.In_Flight__Up_In_The_Air___1_' title='In Flight (Up In The Air, #1) by R.K. Lilley' rel='nofollow noopener'>In Flight</a> first – I can highly recommend it. If you like hot, dominant alpha males, it will definitely work for you. Also, my review may be slightly spoilery for In Flight so please make sure you’ve read that before you carry on here.<br/><br/>We pick up a few weeks after the end of the first book. Bianca has recove</span>
  <span id="freeText2506069595485050908" style="display:none">This is another deeply erotic and highly emotional instalment in Bianca and James' story.<br><br>It's the second part of the Up in the Air Trilogy and it doesn’t work as a standalone. You need to read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16134782.In_Flight__Up_In_The_Air___1_" title="In Flight (Up In The Air, #1) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">In Flight</a> first – I can highly recommend it. If you like hot, dominant alpha males, it will definitely work for you. Also, my review may be slightly spoilery for In Flight so please make sure you’ve read that before you carry on here.<br><br>We pick up a few weeks after the end of the first book. Bianca has recovered slowly from her injuries and is keeping James at a distance and is now back at work flying and is on a night stop in Florida. James is desperate to see her again and will do almost anything to get her back. She does eventually agree to meet him when she is back in Vegas.<br><br>Once she sees him again, she knows she is powerless to resist his charm, the deep attraction that they share is all-consuming and they are soon reunited. We’re starting to see two sides to James Cavendish. There is James, doting, caring boyfriend – he will do everything and anything for Bianca, he thinks of everything, tends to her every need. He worries about her constantly, fears for her safety and there’s a sad vulnerability to him. His feelings for Bianca run so deep but his fear that she will not return his feelings and leave him again is all too apparent.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote> I love any touch from you. It feels caring, and I want that. I want so much for you to care for me.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>The other side of this man is Mr Cavendish – a very much in control dominant. Their BDSM scenes together in this one are simply delicious and quite a lot edgier as they play a little harder in their dungeon on the Fourth Floor than they did in the previous book.<br><br>I think this was so well done – the second book in the trilogy is traditionally very difficult to write and often the most criticised. It’s neither a beginning nor an end and can often just be filler but R.K. Lilley does a really good job of maintaining the integrity of the characters while allowing us to get deeper inside their personalities, all the while moving the story along at a believable pace. Their chemistry is still positively volcanic, the romance a little sweeter and I felt everything with them – their overwhelming desire for each other, their desperation and fear that this won’t work out and, although neither will say it, their obvious love.<br><br> Everyone’s relationships progress further with this one, including Stephan’s and the secrets in Bianca’s past rear their ugly head once again. I think it’s beautifully done, it doesn’t feel rushed, you can feel the intensity growing between Bianca and James, even if neither of them will actually say the words. I am rooting for them to find their HEA, to find an equilibrium that will suit their reticent personalities.<br><br>We end on a moment of drama, while not quite the cliffhanger we had in In Flight, this sets up the final part of the trilogy beautifully. Grounded will finish this story off and, at the time of writing, is currently slated for release on February 26 2013. I can’t wait.<br><br>4 stars BDSM romance<br><br>Oh Mr Cavendish<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397727i/767676._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>

  <span id="freeText3520672011405580908" style="display:none">I was really looking forward to reading this second book in this series. <div id="review_457839678" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/457839678" />
    <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads"><img alt="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578074503p2/8524618.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/457839678?book_show_action=true">Nov 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads">Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer457839678" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16061011437657543653"><b>4 SINFUL JAMES CAVENDISH STARS</b><br/><br/>This is the second book in the Up In The Air Trilogy the first being In Flight which I have to say I didn’t love but don't hate either. I had serious mixed feelings about the book and the series but there was something that made me want to keep going and see how things developed and turned out and I have to say I’m <b>SOOOOO</b> glad I kept reading. This book was freaking <b>SCORCHING...WOWZERS!!!</b> James was extremely delicious in this one with a soft side that I found really </span>
  <span id="freeText16061011437657543653" style="display:none"><b>4 SINFUL JAMES CAVENDISH STARS</b><br><br>This is the second book in the Up In The Air Trilogy the first being In Flight which I have to say I didn’t love but don't hate either. I had serious mixed feelings about the book and the series but there was something that made me want to keep going and see how things developed and turned out and I have to say I’m <b>SOOOOO</b> glad I kept reading. This book was freaking <b>SCORCHING...WOWZERS!!!</b> James was extremely delicious in this one with a soft side that I found really attractive. The writing in the beginning did drag some and there were a couple eye rolling parts but for the most part once I reached the horseback riding scene <i>
  <b>(and NO I will not tell you how that scene turns out but HOLY FREAKING SH*TBALLS it’s MIND FLIPPING BLOWING!! I mean seriously that is probably one of the most creative things I have E.V.E.R read)</b>
</i> I fell in love with it. <br><br>Can I just mention again the horseback riding thing because......<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397931ra/768458.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>WOW</b>...does it make you go <b>
  <i>YES, YES, YES, YES!</i>
</b><br><br>I think this book unraveled so much better than the first. I got more of James in it and felt connected to him and Bianca more. Their chemistry is absolutely palpable as well as the BDSM element came through wayyyy more in this book than the last. I actually really loved the BDSM that was in it. It wasn't too much and didn't feel overwhelming. There were a couple times where I felt like the sexual situations were a little unrealistic but IMO it's fiction which makes the unrealistic situations okay...lol. <br><br><i>
  <b>“I don't feel alone with you. I feel like I have a family and a home again. You're my home. All of the dark shadows seem to disappear when we're together.” - James </b>
</i><br><br>This book starts out exactly where the last book left off. Bianca is taking a break from James. She's trying to collect her thoughts and pull herself together. Being with James is scary for her. When she's with him he makes her feel things she's never felt before and more than that she feels this overwhelming connection to him that she's just never felt with any man <i>(I mean he's the only one she's ever felt attracted too so obviously that's HUGE)</i>. James is full on in love with her in this book. He wants her bad and will not stop until he gets everything he needs from her. His feelings for Bianca run extremely deep. So finally she acquiesces and allows herself to meet up with James at a party. Well when they meet up sparks fly and they fall right back into the swing of things relationship wise. James has a ton of work ahead of him trying to get Bianca to open up and see the relationship for what it is. <br><br>What is the relationship you ask??? <br><br>Welllll...I think that their relationship is one dreams are made of. It's something that can stand the test of time if Bianca can allow herself to be loved by James and if James can try to respect her boundaries and love Bianca back the way she needs <i>(which lets be honest he knows <b>EXACTLY</b> how to love her)</i>. <br><br><i>
  <b>Do you even know how crazy that is ?" I asked in the same quiet voice, as though we could be overheard. "I'm nobody, and you're the most extraordinary man I've ever met. I don't deserve you."<br><br>He made a little sound of protest in his throat. “You’re my angel, Bianca. You've exorcised my demons. I don’t have nightmares when I’m with you. I don’t have to work seventy hour work weeks to keep my mind distracted. My life has become more than work and emotionless affairs. You make me a better man.” </b>
</i><br><br>Gahhhhh...that quote just get's to me <b>Every.Freaking.Time!</b><br><br>This book is basically them working through the issues that surfaced at the end of book 1. It's also about them falling in love with each other. It's about how James needs to dominate and protect her and also how Bianca needs that from James. In this book she realizes how much she craves James's love and attention. It's really, really, really good!!! <br><br>Overall I really loved it and I'm <b>DYING</b> to get my hands on Grounded! I think the next book is going to be amazing. For me Mile High was a combination of sex, love and domination. James lit up the pages keeping the reader fully in tune to his dominating ways. Bianca was the perfect submissive learning that with James she's exactly where she's suppose to be. For a sequel I was extremely impressed as I felt as though the author did an amazing job of keeping the story spicy and interesting as well as building and developing the characters at the same time. I'm very happy with it and would absolutely recommend this series. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16061011437657543653" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/534700865?book_show_action=true">Feb 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer534700865" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16974653993326071713">The ending of <i>In Flight</i> was pretty awful and things haven't gotten better. While Bianca's body is healing, her mind, heart, and soul are trying to make sense of what's going on with her and James. Can she really trust him? And more importantly, can she let him in? <br/><br/>When Bianca finally agrees to see James, it's at a nightclub and James hadn't shown up yet. Bianca was opening up and telling some of the other flight attendants about him...<br/><br/><i>“On a scale of one to ten, what was he?” <br/><br/>I sighed. They were </i></span>
  <span id="freeText16974653993326071713" style="display:none">The ending of <i>In Flight</i> was pretty awful and things haven't gotten better. While Bianca's body is healing, her mind, heart, and soul are trying to make sense of what's going on with her and James. Can she really trust him? And more importantly, can she let him in? <br><br>When Bianca finally agrees to see James, it's at a nightclub and James hadn't shown up yet. Bianca was opening up and telling some of the other flight attendants about him...<br><br><i>“On a scale of one to ten, what was he?” <br><br>I sighed. They were not gonna let up. “How would, ‘I want him to f*ck me to death, and he just might’, rate on that scale?”</i><br><br>Of course, James walks up at that exact moment and he wastes no time in letting Bianca know how much he misses her...<br><br><i>“Did you want me to f*ck you in front of all of your co-workers? Because that’s all I can think about, when I see you in that outfit.”</i><br><br><br>~sigh~ But Bianca is just as affected and while they don't go at it right then, there are plenty of extremely steamy scenes. Some are pretty noteworthy, especially the one on horseback which I still couldn't figure out! (Where's a horse when you need one...LOL!) <br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379786889i/488858.jpg" width="250" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br>I think that's really the draw for me, James' intensity and his insatiableness! How many different places and ways can RKL come up with? And I really want to know more about James...not the whats but the whys! <br><br>The time away from Bianca has only made James...<i>more</i>. More jealous, more intense, more brazen and he's finding it hard to hold back...not that he does...much! I was really surprised about the tattoos though. I still can't believe with everything that has gone on they haven't said those three little words. Even though James' actions are shouting them, Bianca still needs that and I have a feeling James does too. <br><br>The drama is still going on with Jules and she's bringing in more people. The charity event and episode in the bathroom was a bit shocking and unfortunately, I'm sure we're not done with her yet. The good thing that came out of that is Lana. I thought she was fantastic and was sooo happy that at least someone was in Bianca's corner.<br><br>There's some new development with Stephan and a new/old romance. I really like him and want him to be happy. I think that both him and Bianca need to have some growth to be able to let others in. I guess it would be nice if they both got that. <br><br>The drama is still going on with Bianca's past and what happened at the end of the last book really amps up at the end of this one. We get some new and interesting information as well as really harsh stuff...and of course, that's where it leaves us hanging. Onto the last one!<br><br><br>Favorite quotes: <br><br>♥ “Nothing in my life has ever felt as perfect as being inside of you.”<br><br>♥ "I was a slut once with my body, but I’ve never been a slut with my heart.”<br><br>♥ “You make me so happy, Bianca. I never knew life could be this good. I’ve been alone for so long, since my parents died, really. But I don’t feel alone with you. I feel like I have a family and a home again. You’re my home. All of the dark shadows seem to disappear when we’re together.”</span>
  <a data-text-id="16974653993326071713" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText18347322619921615235" style="display:none">Well this one went downhill FAST for me.<br /><br />The things that I loved so much about <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16134782.In_Flight__Up_In_The_Air___1_" title="In Flight (Up In The Air, #1) by R.K. I loved Bianca's backbone in the first book. I liked that she stood up for herself and had boundaries when it came to James. In this book, she surrenders as James's sub and her lovely character disappeared. It was a shame.<br /><br />More than anything, the thing that changed for me from book 1 to book 2 is how I felt about the character of James Cavendish. In book one he was so attractive (in every way), in book 2 he became downright creepy. I disliked how he started to treat Bianca. His obsession with her seemed almost scary to me. He controlled her, dressed her, and completely started to suffocate her (literally AND figuratively)...those of you who've read the book know what I'm referring to. There was something not quite right about Mr. Cavendish, and I stopped seeing him as anything other than a really unhealthy man.<br /><br />I won't be continuing with this series.</span>

<div id="review_1496295483" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1496295483" />
    <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole"><img alt="Duchess Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499265843p2/2204947.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1496295483?book_show_action=true">Jan 05, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Duchess Nicole" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole">Duchess Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=3-star-read">3-star-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-bdsm">genre-bdsm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-contemp-romance">genre-contemp-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-bdsm-lite">genre-bdsm-lite</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=new-shelf-omg-drama">new-shelf-omg-drama</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1496295483" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer956463904949668548">I just don't know what I think about this series. I initially started it because I was told that I needed to read this before reading Tristan and Danika's story. I wasn't impressed with book one, and decided to skip the next two and to right to T and D. LOVED T and D so much, I figured I would push through and get all the tidbits about them from the Up in the Air, even if I wasn't exactly diggin' it. Here at the end of book two in the series and I still haven't been introduced to Tristan or Dani</span>
  <span id="freeText956463904949668548" style="display:none">I just don't know what I think about this series. I initially started it because I was told that I needed to read this before reading Tristan and Danika's story. I wasn't impressed with book one, and decided to skip the next two and to right to T and D. LOVED T and D so much, I figured I would push through and get all the tidbits about them from the Up in the Air, even if I wasn't exactly diggin' it. Here at the end of book two in the series and I still haven't been introduced to Tristan or Danika, so I'm wondering where they come into the story. <br /><br />As far as James and Bianca's story goes, it's okay, I guess. I feel like Bianca is being given every opportunity known to man to understand how much James cares about her, and yet she is so ignorant. It just screams juvenile to me. He can flat out tell her to her face that he wants a permanent, lasting, loving relationship with her and in the next paragraph, she's internalizing how she doesn't know how into their relationship he is. It's so obnoxious. I wish the author would have found a better reason for Bianca to have doubts. <br /><br />The BDSM elements aren't too over the top, but they are a bit eye roll inducing at times. I think maybe I'm just over the fluffy BDSM pieces. I've read a handful of authors who really make me believe it, and use that aspect to drag me kicking and screaming deep into a love affair with the genre. Then I real some silly tripe like this and I just...can't...do...it. I don't believe in it with James and Bianca, I just don't. Their weird jealousy thing that starts up in this book is over the top as well and seems contrived to add drama. Each scene set for a possessive issue ends up feeling really awkward.<br /><br />I will for sure read book three. This wasn't terrible. I get why people like it. I really like all of the secondary characters. I'm curious to read Lana's story, if only because I'm hoping it's set in Hawaii. I love that Bianca is a flight attendant. It's just different, and it means that we get to go from New York to Vegas and back again in pages. I love her bestie and their wonderfully supportive relationship. I like that Bianca is striving to stay independent and that it is really important to her that she continue to work and support herself. She's not giving up her own identity to become James' woman. </span>
  <a data-text-id="956463904949668548" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer16474970066156666927"> ****<b>4 MIND-BLOWING stars</b>****<br/><br/><br/><br/><b>"I never thought I'd have the urge to fuck someone to death."</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1296.photobucket.com/user/blhoffma/media/jasedean2_zps3ebdb484.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

<span id="freeTextContainer859335056193823746">I read this series last year and I'm now listening to the audio version so I am leaving a review based off of how I feel a year later and listening to the series all over again.<br/><br/>At risk of repeating myself from my review from the first book in the series, I can't help but start this review to clearly state that this book series is my absolute favorite series out of everything I have read. The clear devotion of James to Bianca is pretty intoxicating. Who wouldn't want a billionaire who could have </span>
  <span id="freeText859335056193823746" style="display:none">I read this series last year and I'm now listening to the audio version so I am leaving a review based off of how I feel a year later and listening to the series all over again.<br /><br />At risk of repeating myself from my review from the first book in the series, I can't help but start this review to clearly state that this book series is my absolute favorite series out of everything I have read. The clear devotion of James to Bianca is pretty intoxicating. Who wouldn't want a billionaire who could have anyone or anything he wants choose you and to choose you 100%? <br /><br />James has lead a very wild life since losing his parents at such a young age to only be abused by a cousin and then later raised by a very emotionally cold aunt. He strikes out as soon as he is 18 and indulges in woman for years until he meets Bianca. His experience with his cousin has made him need absolute control. BDSM is where he gets that control but he has very few people in his life he cares for or even trusts.<br /><br />Bianca witnesses her father kill her mother at a very young age and she runs away to save herself, meeting Stefan, who becomes her brother and best friend. Stefan protected her while they lived on the streets and an occasional foster home and has been the only man in her life that has every loved and protected her. She trusts no one else. <br /><br />James having been with so many woman and feeling nothing, knows the minute he lays eyes on Bianca that the feeling he gets actually means something and he will stop at nothing to claim her. Bianca does not make this easy for him. He is the first man who has ever made her feel anything as well but she is so used to keep people at a distance she fights to keep him at arms length while he fights to bond her to him for life. <br /><br />The lengths that James goes to to keep Bianca is crazy and probably completely unrealistic but is also the reason I absolutely adore this book series. To have a man so 100% devoted to you that he will fire any staff members who do not treat her well. To be 100% honest to her no matter how bad it may make him look to prove he is placing his complete trust in her. To accept and take care of Stefan, knowing how much he means to Bianca instead of getting jealous and trying to separate them just because it would be what Bianca wants. You just can't help but fall hard for James Cavendish. How could I not love this series! <br /><br />The audio is also very good. I have limited experience listening to audio books but I can say this narrator has been very good with the accents she's had to impersonate and anytime she has had to impersonate a man's voice, it has not detracted from the story.</span>

  <span id="freeText9736156991216515749" style="display:none"><b>3.5 stars</b><br><br>Long story short, on the whole I enjoyed this book more than the previous one. It’s pretty close to 4 stars. He seems to be making it his mission to take care of her in his own dominant way. However, it bothers me that the moment Bianca is in James’s presence, she loses her independence and her boundaries dissolve.<br> <br>Stephan isn’t in this book as much as the first one, and I missed their fun interactions. <br><br>BDSM is integral to the plot, but I think there’s just way too much sex. I found myself wanting to skip some of the sex scenes. It makes me wonder if their relationship is built on a firm foundation or if it’s primarily sex. This series is a page-turning guilty pleasure, though, so I’m off to read the next book.<br><br><a href="http://readingfrenzyblog.com" target="”_blank”" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_488454069" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/488454069" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/488454069?book_show_action=true">Dec 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=drama">drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=billionaire">billionaire</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer488454069" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15520419206524346416">OMG, James Cavendish, you continue to rock my world! <br/><br/>Continuing on one month after the events of the first book, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16134782.In_Flight__Up_In_The_Air___1_' title='In Flight (Up In The Air, #1) by R.K. Lilley' rel='nofollow noopener'>In Flight</a>, this book picks up the drama straight away, with James and Bianca still struggling with their tumultuous, fledgling relationship. They still want each other, badly, but Bianca still has issues with the relationship side. And OMG, those issues get played out in frustrating detail!!!! The woman did my head in for half of this book! How can she still be so freaking oblivious??</span>
  <span id="freeText15520419206524346416" style="display:none">OMG, James Cavendish, you continue to rock my world! <br /><br />Continuing on one month after the events of the first book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16134782.In_Flight__Up_In_The_Air___1_" title="In Flight (Up In The Air, #1) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">In Flight</a>, this book picks up the drama straight away, with James and Bianca still struggling with their tumultuous, fledgling relationship. They still want each other, badly, but Bianca still has issues with the relationship side. And OMG, those issues get played out in frustrating detail!!!! The woman did my head in for half of this book! How can she still be so freaking oblivious??? <br /><br />OK, this isn’t really a spoiler, but there is some major ranting ahead so up to you whether you choose to witness my meltdown… <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br /><br />She doubts James’ intentions even though everything he does and says demonstrates how special she is to him and that he wants a future with her. And she still thinks she’s a casual fling! And then she has the audacity to wonder why HE is insecure about their relationship! BECAUSE YOU REFUSE TO TALK ABOUT IT, YOU STUPID WOMAN!!! THE POOR GUY HAS NO IDEA WHERE HE STANDS!<br /><br />Ugh! I was so mad at her, and then my heart broke even more for James when he says this line… <br /><br /><i> “I love any touch from you. It feels caring, and I want that. I want so much for you to care for me” </i><br /> <br />And. Still. She. Says. Nothing!!!!!!!! Poor James!!! *sob*.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />But James loves her deeply, and storms on regardless, never doubting that he will bring her around. Lavishing her with love, affection and gifts… as well as other things that she needs *wink*. And I must say that through all of my irritation, I never actually really disliked Bianca. I was frustrated with her, sure, but she was honest with herself, and managed to give enough to James to let him know that she was affected by him. And thankfully, she does manage to have an epiphany, and even though she still has issues, she at least grows enough to be more confident and secure with James. Phew!<br /><br />Anyway, complaints about stupid heroine behaviour aside, I did really love this book. James is just amazing. Still controlling and dominant, he mainly keeps it restricted to the bedroom, although he is bossy and involves himself in Bianca’s life in any way that he can. But, this is fiction, it’s expected from him, and we love it! And he seems to know what she needs. While some of their behaviour together may seem a bit weird and OTT (with the undressing, and bathing, and then there’s the other side with the punishment side of things), it works for them. He needs to care for her like that, and she seems to need it (she certainly enjoys it), so who am I to judge? He is, in all ways, generous and loving with Bianca and I love that he introduced some teasing into their relationship. And of course, he is absolutely protective of his girl. <br /><br /><i>“Meet my future. Her name is Bianca. Come to terms with it. My advice would be to get on her good side.”</i><br /><br />Like the first book, there are lots of steamy moments, and even more swoon as James and Bianca start to open up more and more to each other, and James starts to make plans for their future. And, importantly, there is a new level of honesty to their relationship (particularly with James being willing to share details of his sordid past), and I really loved that!<br /><br /><i>“I can’t change my past, Bianca. All I can do is be honest with you, and I’ve done my best.”<br /><br />“I want to deserve you, my love.”</i><br /><br />The dramas continue with Bianca’s family and James’ exes, and with particular storylines left undone and twists uncovered, I’m looking forward to seeing further developments in the next book (including a very well deserved smackdown that I am practically drooling to see!). But mostly, I’m looking forward to seeing Bianca completely let go, and seeing her and James finally getting the HEA that was hinted at in the final pages. <br /><br /><i>“I don’t know how it happened so fast, but you feel like home to me, James.”<br />A hoarse, pained sound escaped his throat. “Yes,” he said, his voice rough with emotion. “This is home.”</i><br /><br />4.5 swoony, steamy stars :)<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15520419206524346416" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

Lilley' rel='nofollow noopener'>In Flight</a><br/><br/>The whole flight crew, including captain Damien, are on an overnight layover in Miami and Bianca is slowly recovering from the assault of her father. Having not seen James for all this time James is on the edge to see her or even talk to her. He begs her to see him and she relents to a meeting in Las Vegas during an outing with the crew. As soon as sh</span>
  <span id="freeText9073605585228541675" style="display:none"><i>There’s no room in perfection for insecurity</i><br><br>Mile High, book 2 of the Up In The Air series, begins almost a month after the end of book 1, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16134782.In_Flight__Up_in_the_Air___1_" title="In Flight (Up in the Air, #1) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">In Flight</a><br><br>The whole flight crew, including captain Damien, are on an overnight layover in Miami and Bianca is slowly recovering from the assault of her father. Having not seen James for all this time James is on the edge to see her or even talk to her. He begs her to see him and she relents to a meeting in Las Vegas during an outing with the crew. As soon as she sees him again she knows she will be not able to resist him.<br><br><i>“Are you punishing me, Mr. Cavendish?” <br>“Of course I am, just to give you a taste. I was desperate for you. To comfort you, to tend to you. Hell, just to look at you. But you withdrew from me completely, until I was pathetically grateful for just a text from you, and even that you withheld most of the time. So I needed to give you at least a small taste of the wanting.”</i><br><br>James whisked her away to his horse ranch, where they have wickedly hot sex on James’s horse, Devil or Demon the verdict on his name is still out!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487714410i/22044227.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>“You must know by now that I’ve never done any of this for anyone else. I was a slut once with my body, but I’ve never been a slut with my heart.”<br><br>Their relationship moves forward in a fast pace with Bianca agreeing to let James take care of her and moving in with him, even agreeing to the round the clock security on her. James showers her with expensive clothing and diamonds. <br>I enjoyed reading how they interact with each other, how they loved everything about each other without voicing the apparently much needed “I love you”, and James even locking the collar. <br><br>We also get to know both his sides: Mr. Beautiful who is tender, loving, caring and jealous. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487714373i/22044222.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And also Mr. Cavendish who is cold, dominant, distant and temperamental, being the master of his 4th floor dungeon. Their scenes in the dungeon were hot but I absolutely did not like the choking scene at the spa, to me it was very alarming.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487714373i/22044223.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> “You’re my angel, Bianca. You’ve exorcized my demons. I don’t have nightmares when I’m with you. I don’t have to work seventy hour work weeks to keep my mind distracted. My life has become more than work and emotionless affairs. You make me a better man.”</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487714373i/22044224.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Book 2 also ends on a cliffy with Bianca getting extremely disturbing news. <br><br>Part of the Up in the Air series that has to be read in order:<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16134782.In_Flight__Up_in_the_Air___1_" title="In Flight (Up in the Air, #1) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer6255252794560412695"><b>SO FREAKING GOOD!</b><br/><br/><i>Mile High</i> is the second book in <i>Up in the Air</i> series. It's still about the amazing love between Bianca and James. If you've ever read <i>Fifty Shades of Grey</i>, this book is better (in my eyes). The chemistry is amazing between these two. They both have pasts that they need help to deal with. Both dealing with abusive men. <br/><br/>The amount of caddy bitches doubles in this book.   <span id="freeText6255252794560412695" style="display:none"><b>SO FREAKING GOOD!</b><br /><br /><i>Mile High</i> is the second book in <i>Up in the Air</i> series. It's still about the amazing love between Bianca and James. If you've ever read <i>Fifty Shades of Grey</i>, this book is better (in my eyes). The chemistry is amazing between these two. They both have pasts that they need help to deal with. Both dealing with abusive men. <br /><br />The amount of caddy bitches doubles in this book. Everyone is out for Bianca's blood because they have no idea what the hell James sees in her. How about her heart ya gold-digging whores? James is even more controlling in this book because of Bianca's safety. He has had enough of everyone's bullshit and to top it all off, he has to worry about her murdering dad. <br /><br />There were some twists and turns in this book, a lot I didn't see coming. A bit like the ending, but I did end up assuming something mysterious happened before I actually heard the ending. After that shit hitting the fan, I am even more pumped to dive into the third book. I'm trying to hard to save the book for tomorrow.. TRYING... SO ... FREAKING.... HARD. </span>

  <img src='https://www.goodreads.com/assets/nocover/60x80.png' alt='Rock Bottom (Tristan & Danika, #2) by R.K. Lilley' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a></span>
  <span id="freeText12812355011208899732" style="display:none"><b>WOW!!!!</b><br><br>Mr. Cavendish doesn't disappoint in this book. There were so many moments where I wanted to jump into the book and take Bianca's place. <br><br><i>"Then live with me. Be with me. Swear you'll never leave me."<br>"I want to lay the world at your feet." <br>"Meet my future"<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/419323.gif" width="240" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Looking forward to book 3 and HEA<br></i><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16134782.In_Flight__Up_In_The_Air___1_" title="In Flight (Up In The Air, #1) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1358794734s/16134782.jpg" alt="In Flight (Up In The Air, #1) by R.K. Lilley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16136959.Mile_High__Up_In_The_Air___2_" title="Mile High (Up In The Air, #2) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1352489991s/16136959.jpg" alt="Mile High (Up In The Air, #2) by R.K. Lilley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16139641.Grounded__Up_In_The_Air___3_" title="Grounded (Up In The Air, #3) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1358701028s/16139641.jpg" alt="Grounded (Up In The Air, #3) by R.K. Lilley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Cliffhangers.<br><br><i>Spinoffs:</i><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17406142.Lana" title="Lana by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1361471750s/17406142.jpg" alt="Lana by R.K. Lilley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17377032.Bad_Things__Tristan___Danika___1_" title="Bad Things (Tristan &amp; Danika, #1) by R.K. Lilley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1371404883s/17377032.jpg" alt="Bad Things (Tristan &amp; Danika, #1) by R.K. Lilley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('rC6eYwB2nS5f6OMXwaVpnZnSv8AuZddKLXuCeTbgHUzfy4CJOlZZrPpDiNO7lMfImPzV2CnYwU0CX3JRmsDR1w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('i+SyWBBy91ATTqr3OCHLATixHDGhtiD2kCNPZetCGQL4AayyKlIz0rblwTNCEGVUOZ92KaYLNvG/B79NR2LVmQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer373823588163343476">R.K. Lilley has been a writer since she can remember, but has held down some interesting jobs to pay the bills. For several years she was a first class flight attendant, and she always swore that she just had to write a book about it. Mixing her love of romance and all things BDSM, the Up In the Air Trilogy is her debut into the world of contempary romance and erotica. She is currently working on </span>
  <span id="freeText373823588163343476" style="display:none">R.K. Lilley has been a writer since she can remember, but has held down some interesting jobs to pay the bills. For several years she was a first class flight attendant, and she always swore that she just had to write a book about it. Mixing her love of romance and all things BDSM, the Up In the Air Trilogy is her debut into the world of contempary romance and erotica. She is currently working on the final installment in the series.<br />You can contact R.K. at Authorrklilley@gmail.com<br />Visit her Facebook page to keep up-to-date on what she's working on<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/authorrklilley">https://www.facebook.com/authorrklilley</a><br /><br />And check out her website <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.rklilley.com/">http://www.rklilley.com/</a><br /><br />R.K. also writes urban fantasy under the pseudonym: Rebecca K.
